add_namespace = rcmchina
# HPC Japan demand independent HPC
country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.1
	title = rcmchina.1.t
	desc = rcmchina.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { CHI = { set_global_flag = marco_polo } }
	option = { #
		name = rcmchina.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 55
			modifier = {
				factor = 60
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			JAP = { country_event = { days = 5 id = rcmjapan.1 } }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = { country_event = { days = 5 id = rcmjapan.1 } }
		}
	}
	option = { #
		name = rcmchina.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 45
			modifier = {
				factor = 40
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		HPC = {
			country_event = { days = 5 id = hpc.2 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = if_they_accept
		effect_tooltip = {
			JAP = {
				country_event = { id = rcmjapan.2 }
			}
			JAP = {
				give_guarantee = HPC
			}
		}
	}
}

# Mao is gaining ground, loses his Cornered Fox trait
country_event = { #guo
	id = rcmchina.5
	title = rcmchina.5.t
	desc = rcmchina.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
		OR = {
		num_of_controlled_states > 6
		NOT = { has_idea = PRC_Isolated_status }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.5.a
		remove_country_leader_trait = desperate_gambit
		#remove_country_leader_trait = cornered_fox
		#remove_ideas = one_last_stand
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = 0.025
		add_war_support = 0.025
		custom_effect_tooltip = gain_base_supp_cond_p10_tt
		add_to_variable = {
		    var = This.supply_condition
			value = 10 #MODDED
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = This.supply_condition_base
			value = 10 #MODDED
		}
	}
}
# Kuomintang Offensive
country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.6
	title = rcmchina.6.t
	desc = rcmchina.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 100
	}
	trigger = {
		always = no
		tag = CHI
		NOT = { has_global_flag = nineteen_thirtynine_start }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = CHI_attack_comm }
		NOT = { has_war_with = PRC }
		any_neighbor_country = {
			tag = PRC
			has_opinion_modifier = hostile_status
		}
	}
	immediate = { set_country_flag = CCW_offensive_executed }
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.6.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = rcmchina.6.tt
			random_list = {
				70 = {
					country_event = { id = rcmchina.9 days = 1 }
					add_political_power = 200
					add_manpower = -10000
				}
				30 = {
					country_event = { id = rcmchina.10 days = 1 }
					add_political_power = -100
					add_manpower = -50000
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = rcmchina.6.tt_2
			country_event = { id = rcmchina.8 days = 1 }
			add_political_power = 100
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			PRC = {
				set_country_flag = CCW_major_attack
				country_event = { id = rcmchina.7 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.6.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = rcmchina.6.tt
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					country_event = { id = rcmchina.9 days = 1 }
					add_political_power = 100
					add_manpower = -1000
				}
				50 = {
					country_event = { id = rcmchina.10 days = 1 }
					add_political_power = -50
					add_manpower = -5000
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = rcmchina.6.tt_2
			country_event = { id = rcmchina.8 days = 1 }
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			PRC = {
				set_country_flag = CCW_medium_attack
				country_event = { id = rcmchina.7 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.6.c
		effect_tooltip = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = rcmchina.6.tt
			random_list = {
				30 = {
					country_event = { id = rcmchina.9 days = 1 }
					add_political_power = 50
					add_manpower = -100
				}
				70 = {
					country_event = { id = rcmchina.10 days = 1 }
					add_political_power = -25
					add_manpower = -500
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = rcmchina.6.tt_2
			country_event = { id = rcmchina.8 days = 1 }
			add_political_power = 25
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			PRC = {
				set_country_flag = CCW_minor_attack
				country_event = { id = rcmchina.7 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.7
	title = rcmchina.7.t
	desc = rcmchina.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.7.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 80 }
		effect_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					country_event = { id = rcmchina.11 }
					add_political_power = -75
					add_manpower = -5000
				}
				50 = {
					country_event = { id = rcmchina.12 }
					add_political_power = 150
					add_manpower = -1000
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CCW_major_attack }
				CHI = {
					random_list = {
						70 = {
							country_event = { id = rcmchina.9 }
						}
						30 = {
							country_event = { id = rcmchina.10 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CCW_medium_attack }
				CHI = {
					random_list = {
						50 = {
							country_event = { id = rcmchina.9 }
						}
						50 = {
							country_event = { id = rcmchina.10 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CCW_minor_attack }
				CHI = {
					random_list = {
						30 = {
							country_event = { id = rcmchina.9 }
						}
						70 = {
							country_event = { id = rcmchina.10 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.7.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		CHI = { country_event = { id = rcmchina.8 days = 1 } }
		add_political_power = -50
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.8
	title = rcmchina.8.t
	desc = rcmchina.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.8.a
		if = {
			limit = { PRC = { has_country_flag = CCW_major_attack } }
			add_political_power = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = { PRC = { has_country_flag = CCW_medium_attack } }
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = { PRC = { has_country_flag = CCW_minor_attack } }
			add_political_power = 25
		}
		PRC = {
			clr_country_flag = CCW_major_attack
			clr_country_flag = CCW_medium_attack
			clr_country_flag = CCW_minor_attack
		}
	}
}

# Border War
country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.13
	title = rcmchina.13.t
	desc = rcmchina.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		always = no #nah
		NOT = { has_global_flag = CHI_Encirclement_Campaign_focus }
		has_country_flag = CCW_offensive_executed
		has_opinion_modifier = hostile_status
		OR = {
			divisions_in_state = {
				state = 744
				size > 0
			}
			divisions_in_state = {
				state = 1030
				size > 0
			}
		}
		PRC = {
			divisions_in_state = {
				state = 622
				size > 0
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 21
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			PRC = { country_event = { id = rcmchina.18 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.13.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					divisions_in_state = {
						state = 744
						size > 0
					}
					divisions_in_state = {
						state = 1030
						size > 0
					}
				}
			}
			744 = { set_border_war = yes }
		}
		622 = { set_border_war = yes }
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.13.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		add_political_power = -50
	}
}
# CHI loses Border War
country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.14
	title = rcmchina.14.t
	desc = rcmchina.14.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			744 = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_border_conflict = yes }
					set_border_war = no
				}
			}
			1030 = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_border_conflict = yes }
					set_border_war = no
				}
			}
			622 = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_border_conflict = yes }
					set_border_war = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.14.a
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = -0.05
		PRC = { country_event = { id = rcmchina.15 } }
	}
}

	desc = rcmchina.18.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = rcmchina.18.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			622 = { set_border_war = yes }
			CHI = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							divisions_in_state = {
								state = 744
								size > 0
							}
							divisions_in_state = {
								state = 1030
								size > 0
							}
						}
					}
					744 = { set_border_war = yes }
					1030 = { set_border_war = yes }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
# Japan attacks - Chinese Popular Front forms
country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.100
	title = rcmchina.100.t
	desc = rcmchina.100.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {  #this is to separate "emergency truce" scenario and regular united front scenario
			AND = {
				is_subject = no
				NOT = { is_ally_with = JAP }
				any_enemy_country = {
					is_subject = no
					NOT = { #prevent zhang lan
						tag = event_target:CDL_JAP_puppet
					}
					NOT = { is_ally_with = JAP }
					NOT = {
						original_tag = PREV
					}
					NOT = {
						is_ally_with = ROOT
					}
					is_literally_china = yes
					NOT = {
						tag = MAN
						tag = ECA
						tag = EHB
						tag = RFM
						tag = CCP
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.100.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_in_faction = yes }
			}
			create_faction = chinese_united_front
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				HPC = {
					exists = yes
				}
				NOT = {
					HPC = {
						is_subject_of = JAP
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_faction = HPC
			add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = HPC enemy = JAP }
		}
		set_global_flag = JAP_attacks_CHI_unites
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				is_warlord = yes
				NOT = {
					tag = SIK
				}
				NOT = {
					tag = ROOT
					AND = {
						OR = {
							tag = HMI
							tag = TNG
						    tag = KHR
						}
						has_war_with = SIK
					}
					OR = {
						tag = KRS
						tag = ATM
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = china101_fired }
				#has_global_flag = JAP_attacks_CHI_unites
				OR = {
					HPC = {
						has_war_with = JAP
					}
					event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
						has_war_with = JAP
					}
					AND = {
						HPC = {
							is_puppet_of = JAP
						}
						event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
							has_war_with = JAP
						}
					}
				}
				#JAP = { has_offensive_war = yes }
				NOT = {
					is_subject_of = JAP
				}
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_faction = no
					owns_state = 614
					tag = SHD
					tag = NEA
				}
				OR = {
					has_war = no
					has_war_with = JAP
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = rcmchina.101 }
		}
	}
}
# Japan attacks - Chinese Popular Front forms( to warlords )
country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.101
	title = rcmchina.101.t
	desc = rcmchina.101.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = china101_fired
	}

	option = { #join united front (Szechwan)
		name = rcmchina.101.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = SHX_Support_north_china_buffer_state_strategy
				is_subject = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				AND = {
					TAG = SIC
					has_government = FROM
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				ROOT = {
					get_current_government_type = yes
				}
				add_to_faction = ROOT
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomous_state = autonomy_dominion
					freedom_level = 0.1
				}
				ROOT = {
					restore_previous_government_type = yes
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = stop_subject_war_end_tt
		add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = FROM enemy = JAP }
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = { id = rcmchina.106 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {#join united front (no puppet, default)
		name = rcmchina.101.g
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = hunan_didnt_stand_with_central_flag
			}
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = SHX_Support_north_china_buffer_state_strategy
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = tng_wants_to_join_the_war
				}
				OR = {
					TAG = HPC
					TAG = HMI
					TAG = KHR
					TAG = TNG
					#TAG = SHD
					TAG = NEA
					TAG = SIC
				    TAG = XIA #
					TAG = KRS
					TAG = ATM
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			add_to_faction = ROOT
		}
		add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = FROM enemy = JAP }
		hidden_effect = {

		}

	}

				targeted_alliance = PREV

			}
		}

		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = chinese_sov_rep_dissolves

					NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }

			}
		}
	}
	#Nothing
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		name = rcmchina.104.b
	}

		NOT = { has_country_flag = nbtz_fired }
		event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = { has_country_flag = china101_fired }
		has_global_flag = china_split
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = JAP
			has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
		}
		event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = { has_war_with = PRC }
		#event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = { owns_state = 1008 }
		event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0

	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = nbtz_fired
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = XIK
					original_tag = YUN
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = dont_want_to_help
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.215.a
		ai_chance ={
			factor = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = joins_CHI
		custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
		effect_tooltip = {
			CHI = { annex_country = { target = ROOT transfer_troops = yes }	}
		}
		hidden_effect = { CHI = { country_event = { days = 2 id =  rcmchina.214 } } }
	}
	option = {
		name =  rcmchina.215.b
		ai_chance ={
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = dont_want_to_help
			}
		}
		add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader enemy = PRC }
	}
	option = {

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				factor = 100

country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.217
	title = rcmchina.217.t
	desc = {
		text = rcmchina.217.d
		trigger = {
			tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rcmchina.217.d_chi
		trigger = {
			tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_civil_war
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		trigger = {
			tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
		}
		name = rcmchina.217.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = XIK
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = all_of_their_units_join_us_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						tag = SIC
						tag = YUN
					}	
					
				}
			}
			annex_country = { target = FROM transfer_troops = yes }
		}
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = XIK
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = all_of_their_units_join_prc_tt
			annex_country = { target = XIK transfer_troops = no }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						country_exists = SIC
					}
				}
				transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = event_target:WTT_communist_china          # the recipient
					size = 0       # [0,1] Default value for the ratio below if they are not specified
					army_ratio = 0.25       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for army
					stockpile_ratio = 0.15  # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for the stockpiled equipment and fuel
					#navy_ratio = 0.2       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for navy
					#air_ratio = 0.4        # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for air
					keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { # Trigger for unit leaders to remain with the original country
						always = yes
					}
				}
			}	
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character = SIC_Pan_Wenhua
				}
				retire_character = SIC_Pan_Wenhua 
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character = SIC_Deng_Xihou
				}
				retire_character = SIC_Deng_Xihou
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = YUN
				}
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				event_target:WTT_communist_china = { annex_country = { target = YUN transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = NXM
				}
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				event_target:WTT_communist_china = { annex_country = { target = NXM transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = SUY
				}
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				event_target:WTT_communist_china = { annex_country = { target = SUY transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
		}
		name = rcmchina.217.b
	}
}

#NO LONGER UNITED (to CHI)
country_event = {
	id = RCM_chinese_civil_war.1
	title = RCM_chinese_civil_war.1.t
	desc = {
		text = RCM_chinese_civil_war.1.d_PRC_joined
		trigger = {
			event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
				has_country_flag = PRC_joined_CHI_against_JAP
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = RCM_chinese_civil_war.1.d_PRC_refused
		trigger = {
			event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = PRC_joined_CHI_against_JAP }
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty1

	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = CHI_no_longer_united_flag
	}
	trigger = {
		#country_exists = event_target:WTT_communist_china
		tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
		is_faction_leader = yes
		any_allied_country = {
			is_literally_china = yes
			is_subject = no
		}
		has_global_flag = JAP_attacks_CHI_unites
		HPC = { NOT = { has_war_with = JAP } }
		SHX = { NOT = { has_war_with = JAP } }
		NOT = { has_war_with = JAP }
		event_target:WTT_communist_china = { NOT = { has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader } }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}

	option = {
		name = RCM_chinese_civil_war.1.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_opinion_modifier = CHI_prc_pact
			}
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = event_target:WTT_communist_china modifier = CHI_prc_pact }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_opinion_modifier = unstable_alliance
			}
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = event_target:WTT_communist_china modifier = unstable_alliance }
		}
		dismantle_faction = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
						exists = yes
					}
				}
				event_target:WTT_communist_china = { country_event = { id = RCM_chinese_civil_war.6 } } #Communist no longer united
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #join nationalists
		name = RCM_chinese_civil_war.8.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_puppet = no
				OR = { #join commies
					has_country_flag = cooperation_with_communist_flag
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_government = communism
							has_government = n_socialism
						}
						has_country_flag = CHI_opposition_flag
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = { #stay out
					has_government = fascism
					has_country_flag = CHI_opposition_flag
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 25
				AND = { #join
					tag = SHC
					has_character = NEA_deng_baoshan
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
			event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
				ROOT = {
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = PREV
						enemy = PREV.PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #you are defecting! people trust you less
			limit = {
				is_puppet = no
				OR = { #join commies
					has_country_flag = cooperation_with_communist_flag
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_government = communism
							has_government = n_socialism
						}
						has_country_flag = CHI_opposition_flag
					}
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -50
			add_war_support = -0.05
			else = {
				add_war_support = 0.05
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #join commies
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				is_puppet = no
				OR = { #join commies
					has_country_flag = cooperation_with_communist_flag
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_government = communism
							has_government = n_socialism
						}
						has_country_flag = CHI_opposition_flag
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = { #stay out
					has_government = fascism
					has_country_flag = CHI_opposition_flag
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = { #stay out
					tag = SHC
					has_character = NEA_deng_baoshan
				}
			}
		}
		name = RCM_chinese_civil_war.8.b
		event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
			event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
				ROOT = {
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = PREV
						enemy = PREV.PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = { #you are defecting! people trust you less
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_puppet = yes					
				}
				OR = { #join commies
						has_country_flag = cooperation_with_nationalist_flag
						AND = {
							OR = {
								has_government = fascism
								has_government = neutrality
								has_government = democratic
							}
							has_country_flag = CHI_opposition_flag
						}
					}
			}
			add_political_power = -50
			add_war_support = -0.05
			else = {
				add_war_support = 0.05
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #stay out
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				AND = { #stay out
					has_government = fascism
					has_country_flag = CHI_opposition_flag
				}
			}
		}
		name = RCM_chinese_civil_war.8.c

	}

	id = rcmchina.253
	title = rcmchina.253.t
	desc = rcmchina.253.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.253.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		JAP = {
			create_faction = CHI_man_bloc
			hidden_effect = {
				news_event = RCM_news.3
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_puppet_of = JAP
				}
				JAP = {
					add_to_faction = PREV
				}
			}
			add_to_faction = FROM
			add_to_faction = HPC
			unlock_national_focus = JAP_revise_hirota_sangesoku_focus
			add_political_power = 100
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = hostile_status }
		}
		FROM = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = hostile_status }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = FROM
				OR = {
				    is_core_of = MAN
				    state = 745
				}
				#is_manchuria_state = yes
			}
			remove_core_of = FROM
			#remove_from_array = { #prolly not a good idea
			#	global.big_china = THIS
			#}
			#remove_from_array = {
			#	global.small_china = THIS
			#}
			clr_state_flag = china_core_state
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				save_global_event_target_as = RCM_japan_friendly_china
				add_political_power = 120
				swap_ideas = { remove_idea = appeasement_policy add_idea = appeasement_policy_2 }
			}
			country_event = { days = 270 id = rcmchina.287 }
			news_event = { id = RCM_news.3 }
			set_global_flag = CHI_accept_san_hiro
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = NEA
				}
				NEA = {
					country_event = rcmchina_pro_jap.1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.272
	title = rcmchina.272.t
	desc = rcmchina.272.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chennault
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
		has_character = CHI_claire_chennault #otherwise it may crash
		date > 1937.6.8
		NOT = { has_global_flag = nineteen_thirtynine_start }
		NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
		NOT = { is_in_faction_with = JAP }
		NOT = { has_government = communism }
		NOT = { has_government = fascism }
	}
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = flying_tiger
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.272.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		trigger = {
			amount_taken_ideas = {
			    amount < 2 #one or more free slot
			    slots = {
				   foreign_advisor
			    }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -80
		add_ideas = CHI_claire_chennault
		#if = {
		#	limit = {
		#		has_idea = joseph_stilwell_chi
		#	}
		#	remove_ideas = joseph_stilwell_chi
		#}
	}
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				amount_taken_ideas = {
				    amount > 1 #no more slot
				    slots = {
					   foreign_advisor
				    }
				}
			}
		}
		name = rcmchina.272.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_foreign_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = CHI_claire_chennault
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.273
	title = rcmchina.273.t
	desc = rcmchina.273.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.273.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				JAP = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = fascism
					}
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war_support < 0.5
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = {
					has_idea = CHI_soong_mei_ling
				}
				factor = 2 #this nice lady wants to buy some fighter planes, who are we to tell her no? So what if she has no money?
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = THIS_IS_HISTORICAL_TT
		set_country_flag = CHI_flying_tigers
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = send_volunteers_desire
			id = FROM
			value = 200
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = support
			id = FROM
			value = 200
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = wtt_news.34 days = 1 }
		}
		unlock_decision_tooltip = CHI_flying_tigers
		event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = { country_event = { id = rcmchina.274 } }
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_ace = { name = "Edward" surname = "Rector" callsign = "Ed" type = fighter_genius is_female = no }
			add_ace = { name = "Robert" surname = "Smith" callsign = "R.T." type = fighter_genius is_female = no }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_flying_tiger_tt
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.273.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		CHI = { country_event = { id = rcmchina.275 } }
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.274.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		add_ace = { name = "Edward" surname = "Rector" callsign = "Ed" type = fighter_genius is_female = no }
		add_ace = { name = "Robert" surname = "Smith" callsign = "R.T." type = fighter_genius is_female = no }
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_flying_tiger_tt
		hidden_effect = {
            if = {
	            limit = { has_dlc = "By Blood Alone" }
		            set_technology = {
				        basic_small_airframe = 1
				        basic_medium_airframe = 1
			        }
	            else = {
                    set_technology = {
				        fighter1 = 1
				        tactical_bomber1 = 1
			        }
	            }
            }					
			if = {
	            limit = { has_dlc = "By Blood Alone" }
		            load_oob = "CHI_flying_tiger_bba"
	            else = {
		            load_oob = "CHI_flying_tiger"
	            }
            }
		}		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.284
	title = rcmchina.284.t
	desc = rcmchina.284.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		#all mainland troops return to home islands
		
		if = { #check if HPC somehow steals the leadership
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				has_country_flag = temp_current_china_leader
				NOT = {
					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				}
			}
			event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
				if = {	limit = { NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
					set_variable = { global.previous_china_leader = THIS }
				}
			}
			clear_global_event_target = WTT_current_china_leader
			save_global_event_target_as = WTT_current_china_leader
		}
	    #hidden_effect = { #remove trigger will do
		#   remove_suiyuan_stronghold = yes
	    #}
	}
	option = {#RELEASE KOR
		name = rcmchina.284.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				MAN = {
					OR = {
						controls_state = 527
						controls_state = 525
						controls_state = 1003
						controls_state = 1004
						controls_state = 1000
						controls_state = 1001
						controls_state = 999
						controls_state = 1002
					}
				}
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = { #send Japan's troops back home
			array = global.big_china
			tooltip = big_china_tt
			teleport_armies = { 
				to_state = 282
				limit = {
					tag = JAP
					# trigger will be checked for owner of armies and will only teleport if true. scope if the owner of the army and prev is the scope that calls teleport_armies
				} 
			}
		}
		KOR = {
			every_owned_state = {
				teleport_armies = { 
					to_state = 282
					limit = {
						tag = JAP
						# trigger will be checked for owner of armies and will only teleport if true. scope if the owner of the army and prev is the scope that calls teleport_armies
					} 
				}
			}
			every_controlled_state = {
				teleport_armies = { 
					to_state = 282
					limit = {
						tag = JAP
						# trigger will be checked for owner of armies and will only teleport if true. scope if the owner of the army and prev is the scope that calls teleport_armies
					} 
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						controls_state = 527
						controls_state = 525
						controls_state = 999
						controls_state = 1000
						controls_state = 1001
						controls_state = 1002
						controls_state = 1003
						controls_state = 1004
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = socialist_korea_flag
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
						has_war_together_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = communist_china_liberates_too_flag
			}
		    if = {
				limit = {
						728 = { is_owned_by = JAP }
					      }
				transfer_state = 728
				}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = this_might_take_a_while_to_load_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = blank_line
		peace_with_japan_land_partition = yes
		KOR = {
			transfer_state = 527 
			transfer_state = 525 
			transfer_state = 999 
			transfer_state = 1000 
			transfer_state = 1001 
			transfer_state = 1002 
			transfer_state = 1003 
			transfer_state = 1004 
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			white_peace = KOR
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT modifier = liberator
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
						has_war_together_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = event_target:WTT_communist_china modifier = liberator
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			KOR = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_global_flag = socialist_korea_flag
					}
					set_popularities = {
						democratic = 10
						fascism = 10
						communism = 10
						n_socialism = 60
						neutrality = 10
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = n_socialism
					}
					else = {
						add_opinion_modifier = {
							target = ROOT modifier = liberator
						}

								has_global_flag = communist_china_liberates_too_flag
							}

								target = event_target:WTT_communist_china modifier = liberator
							}

			}

			country_event = rcmchina_extra.2
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			JAP = {
				remove_from_faction = HPC
				remove_from_faction = CHI
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = this_will_lead_to_war_tt
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina_extra.1.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		JAP = {
			country_event = rcmchina_extra.3
			add_political_power = 25
		}
		add_political_power = -75
		remove_ideas = {
			the_blueshirts
			central_club
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					not_has_appeasement_policy_2 = yes
				}
			}
			appeasement_policy_2_level_up = yes
			else = { #in case of having AP0 or default AP or not at all
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = appeasement_policy_0
					}
					swap_ideas = {
						add_idea = appeasement_policy_2
						remove_idea = appeasement_policy_0
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = appeasement_policy
					}
					swap_ideas = {
						add_idea = appeasement_policy_2
						remove_idea = appeasement_policy
					}
					else = {
						add_ideas = appeasement_policy_2
					}
				}
			}
		}

	}
}

			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = THIS_IS_HISTORICAL_TT

			#}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 25
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		
        if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

					is_ally_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				}
				white_peace = ROOT
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject = no

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

                set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT

				}

		}

			limit = {

					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				}
			}
			WTT_political_struggle_remove_current_country = yes
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
				focus = CHI_new_model_province
			    #uncomplete_children = yes
			    #refund_political_power = no
			}	
		}

			limit = {
				is_legit_china = yes
			}
			country_event = rcmchina.317
		}

				has_government = neutrality
			}

						}
					} 
				} 	
			}
		}

				has_government = democratic
			}
			SIC_Zhong_Tiqian = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {

						}
					} 
				} 	
			}
		}

			}

					promote_leader = yes

			has_war_with = FROM
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = rcmchina.320.t_surrender
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FROM
			}
		}
	}
	desc = rcmchina.320.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_flag
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.320.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		SIC = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_id = 3050
					}
				}
				set_nationality = ROOT
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NDP_unite		
		hidden_effect = {
			annex_country = { target = SIC transfer_troops = yes }
			set_global_flag = joined_chi_SIC
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.321
	title = rcmchina.321.t
	desc = {
		text = rcmchina.321.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_other_country = {
					is_legit_china = yes
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rcmchina.321.d_war
		trigger = {
			any_other_country = {
				is_legit_china = yes
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_liu_xiang
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = SIC
		date > 1937.10.20
		date < 1939.1.1
		SIC = {
			has_government = neutrality
			has_country_leader = { character = SIC_liu_xiang }
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_legit_china = yes
				}
				country_event = rcmchina.330
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.321.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			days = 420
			idea = leader_hospitalized
		}
		effect_tooltip = {

		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.325
	title = rcmchina.325.t
	desc = rcmchina.325.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_fu
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_political_party = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 80
			}
			set_political_party = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 20
			}
			set_political_party = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0
			}
			set_political_party = {
				ideology = n_socialism
				popularity = 0
			}
			set_political_party = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.325.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_country_flag = im_warlord_now
		#save_global_event_target_as = PLM_scope #for political struggle #no need added thru focus
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
			}
			load_focus_tree = { tree = china_warlord_focus keep_completed = yes }
		    #unlock_national_focus = CHI_secure_internal_politics
			#unlock_national_focus = CHI_cooperation_with_the_nationalists
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		    kill_country_leader = yes
		}
		SHX = {   
			SHX_Dong_Qiwu = { set_nationality = PLM }
			SHX_Sun_Lanfeng = { set_nationality = PLM }
			SHX_fu_zuoyi = { set_nationality = PLM }
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			SHX_fu_zuoyi = {        
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = despotism
						traits = { fu_zuoyi_doctrine }            
					} 
				}     						  			
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character = SHX_fu_zuoyi
				}
				SHX_fu_zuoyi = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							expire = "1965.1.1"
							ideology = despotism
							traits = {
								fu_zuoyi_doctrine
							}
						} 
					} 
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							expire = "1965.1.1"
							ideology = marxism
							traits = {
								fu_zuoyi_doctrine
							}
						} 
					}
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							expire = "1965.1.1"
							ideology = n_socialism_ideology
							traits = {
								fu_zuoyi_doctrine
							}
						} 
					}

						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							expire = "1965.1.1"
							ideology = sanmin_military_rule
							traits = {
							   fu_zuoyi_doctrine
						   }
						} 
					}	
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							expire = "1965.1.1"
							ideology = conservatism
							traits = {

							}
						} 
					}					    
				}

				}
				else = {
					create_country_leader = {
						name = SHX_fu_zuoyi
						desc = "POLITICS_FU_ZUOYI_DESC"
						picture = "Portrait_PLM_Fu_Zuoyi.dds"

						}

						name = SHX_fu_zuoyi
						desc = "POLITICS_FU_ZUOYI_DESC"
						picture = "Portrait_PLM_Fu_Zuoyi.dds"

						traits = {
						}

		}

#Emergency peace when Japan declare on us but we have a civil war
country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.331
	title = rcmchina.331.t
	desc = rcmchina.331.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_army_mountainside
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		is_subject = no
		NOT = { is_ally_with = JAP }
		any_enemy_country = {
			is_subject = no
			NOT = { #prevent zhang lan
				tag = event_target:CDL_JAP_puppet
			}
			NOT = { is_ally_with = JAP }
			NOT = {
				original_tag = PREV
			}
			NOT = {
				is_ally_with = ROOT
			}
			is_literally_china = yes
			NOT = {
				tag = MAN
				tag = ECA
				tag = EHB
				tag = RFM
				tag = CCP
			}
		}				
		#NOT = {
		#	any_enemy_country = {
		#		tag = event_target:CDL_JAP_puppet
		#	}
		#}
		#is_subject = no
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			hidden_effect = { #so we can survive
				JAP = {
					add_ideas = japan_debuff_emergent_truce
				}
				set_global_flag = japan_debuffed
			}
		}
	}
	option = {#emergency peace!
		name = rcmchina.331.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_in_faction = yes }
			}
			create_faction = chinese_united_front
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = JAP
				}
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						tag = MAN
					}
					is_literally_china = yes
					has_war_with = JAP
				}
				ROOT = {
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = PREV enemy = JAP
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject = no
				NOT = { #prevent zhang lan
					tag = event_target:CDL_JAP_puppet
				}
				NOT = { is_ally_with = JAP }
				NOT = {
					original_tag = PREV
				}
				NOT = {
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
				is_literally_china = yes
				NOT = {
					tag = MAN
					tag = ECA
					tag = EHB
					tag = RFM
					tag = CCP
				}
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
			country_event = {
				hours = 6 id = rcmchina.332
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = JAP_attacks_CHI_unites
		every_country = { #united front
			limit = {
				is_warlord = yes
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							tag = HMI
							tag = TNG
						    tag = KHR
						}
						has_war_with = SIK
					}
					OR = {
						tag = KRS
						tag = ATM
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = china101_fired }
				#has_global_flag = JAP_attacks_CHI_unites
				OR = {
					HPC = {
						has_war_with = JAP
					}
					any_other_country = {
						is_legit_china = yes
						has_war_with = JAP
					}
					AND = {
						HPC = { is_puppet_of = JAP }
						any_other_country = {
							is_legit_china = yes
							has_war_with = JAP
						}
					}
				}
				#JAP = { has_offensive_war = yes }
				NOT = {
					is_subject_of = JAP
				}
				#any_other_country = {
				#	is_legit_china = yes
				#	NOT = {
				#		has_war_with = ROOT
				#	}
				#}
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_faction = no
					owns_state = 614
					tag = SHD
				}
				OR = {
					has_war = no
					has_war_with = JAP
					has_war_together_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = rcmchina.101 }
		}
	}
	option = {#no thanks
		name = rcmchina.331.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.332
	title = rcmchina.332.t
	desc = rcmchina.332.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japan_army_mountainside
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = japan_debuffed
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = { #so we can survive
				JAP = {
					add_ideas = japan_debuff_emergent_truce
				}
				set_global_flag = japan_debuffed
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #yes
		name = rcmchina.332.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_country_flag = agree_peace_flag
		every_controlled_state = { #divide the land
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			transfer_state_to = ROOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			#every_other_country = {
			#	limit = {
			#		is_ally_with = ROOT
			#	}
			#	white_peace = FROM
			#}
			leave_faction = yes
			#dismantle_faction = yes
			create_wargoal = { #FOR CONTINUE THE CIVIL WAR AFTER THE WAR
				target = FROM
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_faction_leader = no
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		white_peace = FROM
		add_to_war = {
			targeted_alliance = FROM enemy = JAP
		}
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_ally_with = FROM
					is_literally_china = yes
				}
			}
			white_peace = ROOT
		}
		FROM = {
			add_to_faction = ROOT
		}
		#if = {
		#	limit = {
		#		NOT = { has_country_flag = china101_fired }
		#		is_faction_leader = yes
		#	}
		#	country_event = { id = rcmchina.101 }
		#}
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = {
					days = 1 id = rcmchina.333
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.332.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = {
					days = 1 id = rcmchina.334
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = rcmchina.340
	title = rcmchina.340.t
	desc = rcmchina.340.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_tibet

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		name = rcmchina.340.a
		FROM = { country_event = { id = rcmchina.341 days = 7 } }
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		name = rcmchina.340.b
		FROM = { country_event = { id = rcmchina.342 days = 7 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		name = rcmchina.340.b
		FROM = { country_event = { id = rcmchina.343 days = 7 } }
	}
}

#Chinese Demand Outer Mongolia
country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.345
	title = rcmchina.345.t
	desc = rcmchina.345.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_sino_sov_diplomacy

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rcmchina.345.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				FROM = { has_defensive_war = yes }
				strength_ratio = { tag = FROM ratio < 0.25 }
				AND = {
					PRC = { exists = yes }
					PRC = { is_puppet = no }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = rcmchina.345.a_tt
		FROM = {
			create_wargoal = { target = MON type = annex_everything }
			if = {
				limit = { TAN = { exists = yes } }
				create_wargoal = { target = TAN type = annex_everything }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SIK = { exists = yes }
					NOT = { SIK = { is_puppet_of = FROM } }
				}
				create_wargoal = { target = SIK type = annex_everything }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					TAN = { exists = no }
					SOV = { owns_state = 392 }
				}
				create_wargoal = {
					target = SOV
					type = take_state_focus
					generator = { 392 }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = CHI_news.13 days = 7 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = rcmchina.345.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				FROM = { has_war = no }
				strength_ratio = { tag = CHI ratio > 0.5 }
				has_war_with = GER
				has_war_with = ENG
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				strength_ratio = { tag = CHI ratio > 0.75 }
				FROM = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_war_with = ENG
						FROM = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
					}
					AND = {
						has_war_with = GER
						FROM = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		MON = { country_event = { id = rcmchina.346 days = 1} }
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = SIK }
			SIK = { country_event = { id = rcmchina.346 days = 1} }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = TAN }
			TAN = { country_event = { id = rcmchina.346 days = 1} }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				TAN = { exists = no }
				owns_state = 329
			}
			FROM = { transfer_state = 329 }
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = CHI_news.12 days = 7 } }
	}
}

#Mongolia and Tannu receive News of Soviet withdrawl
country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.346
	title = rcmchina.346.t
	desc = rcmchina.346.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_sino_sov_diplomacy
    immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			SOV = {
				set_autonomy = { target = ROOT autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = SOV
			}
			SOV = {
				remove_from_faction = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { TAG = SIK } }
		name = rcmchina.346.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
		event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = { country_event = { id = rcmchina.347 days = 6 } }
	}

	#Puppet option for Humans - SRSLY? Y U DO?
	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { TAG = SIK } }
		name = rcmchina.346.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = { country_event = { id = rcmchina.348 days = 6 } }
	}

	option = {
		trigger = { TAG = SIK }
		name = rcmchina.346.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
		event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = { country_event = { id = rcmchina.349 days = 3 } }
	}

	option = {
		trigger = { TAG = SIK }
		name = rcmchina.346.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = { country_event = { id = rcmchina.350 days = 3 } }
	}
}

country_event = {#second united front
	id = rcmchina.352
	title = rcmchina.352.t
	desc = rcmchina.352.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes


	option = {
		name = rcmchina.352.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = THIS_IS_HISTORICAL_TT
		event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = CHI modifier = CHI_prc_pact
			}
		}
		CHI = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = event_target:WTT_communist_china modifier = CHI_prc_pact
			}
		}
		diplomatic_relation = { country = CHI relation = non_aggression_pact }
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI = {
				country_event = rcmchina.353
				white_peace = event_target:WTT_communist_china
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = CHI
					NOT = { tag = CHI }
				}
				white_peace = event_target:WTT_communist_china
				white_peace = GXC
				white_peace = GUD
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china
					NOT = { tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china }
				}
				white_peace = CHI
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea_with_trait = editor
					has_available_idea_with_traits = { idea = editor limit = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.352.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = xian_incident_flag
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = this_will_lead_to_war_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI = {
				country_event = rcmchina.354
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {#second united front #event_target:WTT_communist_china acce
	id = rcmchina.353
	title = rcmchina.353.t
	desc = rcmchina.353.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rcmchina.353.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = event_target:WTT_communist_china modifier = CHI_prc_pact
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = event_target:WTT_communist_china modifier = CHI_prc_pact
			}
			diplomatic_relation = { country = event_target:WTT_communist_china relation = non_aggression_pact }
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = -30
	}
}

######SECOND CENTRAL PLAIN WAR
country_event = { ###second_central_plains_war
	id = rcmchina.355
	title = rcmchina.355.t
	desc = rcmchina.355.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_02
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.355.a
		trigger = {
			is_faction_leader = no
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					tag = event_target:scp_war_opposition_leader
					tag = event_target:scp_war_old_leader
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.355.b
		trigger = { TAG = event_target:scp_war_opposition_leader }
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_subject_of = event_target:scp_war_old_leader
				}
			}
			end_puppet = FROM
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = no
			}
			create_faction = WRL_leader_generic_faction
			add_to_faction = FROM
			else = {
				add_to_faction = FROM
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = ROOT enemy = event_target:scp_war_old_leader }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina.355.c
		trigger = { TAG = event_target:scp_war_old_leader }
	} #Join opposition faction
}

###second_central_plains_war, generic
country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.358
	title = rcmchina.358.t
	desc = {
		text = rcmchina.358.d
		trigger = {
			event_target:scp_war_opposition_leader = {
				NOT = {
					tag = NEA
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = nea.1.d
		trigger = {
			event_target:scp_war_opposition_leader = {
				tag = NEA
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_flag
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { #join
		name = rcmchina.358.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				add = 70
				tag = SHD
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				is_neighbor_of = event_target:scp_war_opposition_leader
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					tag = XSM
					tag = NXM
					tag = GSM
					tag = EGM
					tag = TNG
					tag = HMI
					tag = CHI
				    tag = KHR
					tag = KRS
					tag = ATM
				}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_war_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china
				ROOT = {
					any_owned_state = {
						has_state_flag = I_choose_this_state_to_DMZ
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china = yes
				}
				white_peace = ROOT
			}
		}
		event_target:scp_war_old_leader = {
			event_target:scp_war_opposition_leader = {
				ROOT = {
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = PREV
						enemy = PREV.PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china
				any_owned_state = {
					has_state_flag = I_choose_this_state_to_DMZ
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				clr_state_flag = I_choose_this_state_to_DMZ
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			white_peace = event_target:WTT_communist_china
			hidden_effect = {
				event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
					white_peace = ROOT
				}
				
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = event_target:scp_war_opposition_leader
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						is_subject_of = event_target:scp_war_old_leader
						has_war_with = PREV
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					white_peace = PREV
				}
			}
			country_event = { days = 1 id = rcmchina.355 }
		}
		event_target:scp_war_old_leader = {
			country_event = { days = 1 id = rcmchina.355 }
		}
		event_target:scp_war_opposition_leader = {
			country_event = { days = 1 id = rcmchina.355 }
		}
	}
	option = { #join #annex
		name = rcmchina.358.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 200
				event_target:scp_war_opposition_leader = {
					tag = NEA
				}
				tag = event_target:scp_war_old_leader
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				event_target:scp_war_opposition_leader = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							tag = NEA
							tag = GXC
						}
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
					}
				}
				is_neighbor_of = event_target:scp_war_opposition_leader
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			event_target:scp_war_opposition_leader = {
				annex_country = {
					target = ROOT transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = event_target:scp_war_opposition_leader
			}
			country_event = { days = 1 id = rcmchina.356 }
		}
		event_target:scp_war_old_leader = {
			country_event = { days = 1 id = rcmchina.356 }
		}
		event_target:scp_war_opposition_leader = {
			country_event = { days = 1 id = rcmchina.356 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
	}
	option = { #join #kmt
		name = rcmchina.358.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 120
				OR = {
					tag = XSM
					#tag = SHX
					tag = NXM
					tag = GSM
					tag = EGM
					tag = YUN
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:scp_war_opposition_leader = {
			event_target:scp_war_old_leader = {
				ROOT = {
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = PREV
						enemy = PREV.PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = event_target:scp_war_opposition_leader
			}
			country_event = { days = 1 id = rcmchina.357 }
		}
		event_target:scp_war_old_leader = {
			country_event = { days = 1 id = rcmchina.357 }
		}
		event_target:scp_war_opposition_leader = {
			country_event = { days = 1 id = rcmchina.357 }
		}
		set_country_flag = joined_kmt_in_civil_war_flag
	}
	option = { #not join
		name = rcmchina.358.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				TAG = event_target:scp_war_old_leader
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = not_join_civil_war_flag
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_global_flag = gud_ready
						GXC = { has_offensive_war_with = event_target:scp_war_old_leader }
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							tag = SHC
							tag = GUD
							tag = GXC
							tag = SIC
							tag = SHD
						}
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				OR = {
					#tag = SHX
					tag = YUN
					tag = HPC
					tag = XIK
					tag = PLM
					tag = XSM
					tag = NXM
					tag = GSM
					tag = EGM
					tag = TNG
					tag = HMI
				    tag = KHR
					tag = KRS
					tag = ATM
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 150
				OR = {
					tag = SHX #MODDED
					tag = TNG
					tag = HMI
				    tag = KHR
					tag = KRS
					tag = ATM
				}
			}
		}

# Notification to WTT_current_china_leader that FROM has gained support and will take over leadership
country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.361
	title = wtt_take_national_leadership.1.t
	desc = wtt_take_national_leadership.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_politicians_captured

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { global.previous_china_leader = THIS }
			save_event_target_as = old_leader
			clr_country_flag = wtt_political_struggle
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = CHI_warlord_leader # warlord has taken over before this happened
						has_cosmetic_tag = CHI_warlord_PRC
						has_cosmetic_tag = CHI_second_republic_red
						has_cosmetic_tag = CHI_second_republic_blue
						has_cosmetic_tag = CHI_second_republic
					}
				}
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = CHI
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_power_struggle_defeated
			}
			FROM = {
				save_event_target_as = new_leader
				CHI_negative_spirit_transfer = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_global_flag = lushan_declaration_flag
					}
					add_country_leader_trait = generallissimo
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = CHI_power_struggle_defeated
					}
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_puppet = no
								has_country_flag = cooperation_with_communist_flag
							}
							set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_warlord_PRC
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								is_puppet = no
								NOT = {
									has_country_flag = CHI_opposition_flag
								}
							}
							set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_warlord_leader
						}
					}
				}
				clear_global_event_target = WTT_current_china_leader #former china not us
				save_global_event_target_as = WTT_current_china_leader
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = china_government_legitimacy
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Accept
	option = {
		clr_global_flag = wtt_national_leadership_takeover_in_progress
		name = wtt_take_national_leadership.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_stability > 0.7
				has_war = no
			}
		}

		every_country = {
			limit = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			FROM = { add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = ROOT enemy = PREV hostility_reason = asked_to_join } }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					set_state_owner = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = {		
				NOT = {	has_id = 5010 }			 
		    }
			set_nationality = FROM
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = wtt_take_national_leadership.2 }
			
			hidden_effect = {
				news_event = { id = wtt_news.45 days = 3 }
			}

			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT transfer_troops = yes
			}
			WTT_political_struggle_recalculate_support = yes

		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
	}

	#Refuse
	option = {

		name = wtt_take_national_leadership.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					has_stability > 0.7
				}
				has_war_with = JAP
				surrender_progress > 0.1
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
					ROOT = { remove_from_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
					remove_from_faction = ROOT
				}
			}

			#End political struggle
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = wtt_political_struggle }
				WTT_political_struggle_pause_current_country = yes
			}
		}


		declare_war_on = { target = FROM type = annex_everything }
		start_civil_war = { #states_filter doesnt work!
		    ideology = communism
		    size = 0.2
		    ###only_own_territory = yes
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = ROOT
				has_war_with = ROOT
				has_government = communism
			}
			every_unit_leader = {
				set_nationality = FROM
			}
			FROM = {
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		    FROM = { 
			    every_unit_leader = {
			        limit = {
				        OR = {
					        has_id = 5010
						    has_id = 5011
						    has_id = 5012
						    has_id = 5013
						    has_id = 5014
							has_id = 5015
							has_id = 2031
					    }
				    }
			        set_nationality = ROOT
		        }
		    }
		    ROOT = {
			    if = { 
				    limit = {
					    NOT = {
							has_country_leader = {
	                            character = CHI_chiang_kai_shek
	                            ruling_only = yes
                            }
					    }
					}
				    kill_country_leader = yes
					#kill_country_leader = yes
			        CHI_chiang_kai_shek = {
			            set_nationality = ROOT
						promote_leader = yes
					}
			    }
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = wtt_war_over_national_leadership
		set_country_flag = wtt_refused_giving_leadership
		clr_global_flag = wtt_national_leadership_takeover_in_progress
		add_ideas = CHI_illegal_regime
		FROM = {
			create_faction = WRL_leader_generic_faction
			country_event = { id = wtt_take_national_leadership.3 }
		}
	}
}

	    trigger = {
			original_tag = MON
		}

		    factor = 100
		}

country_event = {
	id = rcm_warlord_help.1
	title = rcm_warlord_help.1.t
	desc = rcm_warlord_help.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rifles
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rcm_warlord_help.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				FROM = {
					tag = SOV					
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						has_equipment = { 
							infantry_equipment > 59999
						}
					}
				}
				effect_tooltip = {
					FROM = {
						send_equipment = {
							equipment = infantry_equipment
							amount = 6000
							target = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						has_equipment = { 
							infantry_equipment > 29999
						}
					}
				}
				effect_tooltip = {
					FROM = {
						send_equipment = {
							equipment = infantry_equipment
							amount = 3000
							target = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				effect_tooltip = {
					FROM = {
						send_equipment = {
							equipment = infantry_equipment
							amount = 1000
							target = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { #for supporting Ili rebellion
			limit = {
				original_tag = SIK
				NOT = { tag = SIK }				
				FROM = {
					tag = SOV					
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { #send more guns man!
					FROM = {
						has_equipment = {
							infantry_equipment > 59999
						}
					}
				}
				effect_tooltip = {
					FROM = {
						send_equipment = {
							equipment = infantry_equipment
							amount = 4000
							target = FROM
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { #send more guns man!
					FROM = {
						has_equipment = {
							infantry_equipment > 29999
						}
					}
				}
				effect_tooltip = {
					FROM = {
						send_equipment = {
							equipment = infantry_equipment
							amount = 1000
							target = FROM
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { has_manpower > 3000 }
				}
				effect_tooltip = {
					FROM = {
						add_manpower = -3000
					}
					add_manpower = 3000
				}				
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { this.num_battalions < 340 }
						AND = {
							ROOT = { NOT = { has_war_with = JAP } }
							check_variable = { this.num_battalions < 500 }
						}
					}	
					#has_defensive_war = no
					FROM = {
						has_equipment = {
							infantry_equipment > 49999
						}
					}	
				}
				#FROM = {
				#	transfer_units_fraction = {
				#		target = ROOT          # the recipient
				#		size = 0            # [0,1] Default value for the ratio below if they are not specified
				#		army_ratio = 0.05       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for army
				#		#stockpile_ratio = 0.3  # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for the stockpiled equipment and fuel
				#		#navy_ratio = 0.2       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for navy
				#		#air_ratio = 0.4        # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for air
				#		keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { # Trigger for unit leaders to remain with the original country
				#			always = yes
				#		}
				#	}
				#}
				else = {
					effect_tooltip = {
						add_to_variable = {
							var = This.supply_condition_base
							value = 5
						}
					}
				}
			}			
		}
		else = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				FROM = {
					send_equipment = {
						equipment = infantry_equipment
						amount = 1000
						target = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			id = rcmchina.338
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = NW_United_GOV
		CHI = {
			end_puppet = NEA
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = RCM_news.4
			set_global_flag = no_point_to_have_tacit_truce
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = I_choose_this_state_to_DMZ
				}
				clr_state_flag = I_choose_this_state_to_DMZ
			}
			CHI = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = communism size = 0.1
					states_filter = {
						is_owned_by = CHI
					}
					states = { 1016 622 607 620 1043 }
				}
			}	
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = CHI
					NOT = {
						tag = CHI
					}
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = NEA
				}
				NEA = {
					annex_country = {
						target = PREV
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
				}
			}			
			
			NEA = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_id = 5010
							has_id = 5011
						    has_id = 5012
						    has_id = 5013
						    has_id = 5014
							has_id = 5015
							has_id = 2031
						}
					}
					set_nationality = CHI
				}
			}
			
			CHI = {
			    #guo kill_country_leader = yes
			    CHI_chiang_kai_shek = {
			        promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
			
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china = yes
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = JAP
							has_war_together_with = JAP
						}
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = KMT_pro_JAP_NW_alliance_formed_gl
				set_country_flag = KMT_pro_JAP_NW_alliance_formed
				#
			}
			event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
				country_event = {
					days = 2 id = rcmchina_pro_jap.2
				}
			}
			NEA = {
				leave_faction = yes
				declare_war_on = {
					target = CHI
					type = annex_everything
				}	
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CNSP_become_ruling_party_politics_tt
		
		event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
		create_country_leader = {
			name = Xu_Fulin
			desc = ""
			picture = "Portrait_CHI_Xu_Fulin.dds"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = socialism
			traits = { #guo
				fulizhichizhe education_reformer
			}
		}
		set_party_name = {
		    ideology = democratic
		    name = CHI_democratic_party
		    long_name = CHI_democratic_party_long
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.4
		}
		democratize_the_parties = yes#guo
		clear_prvious_election_flags = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				months = 46 id = rcmchina_nomination_convention_future.1
			}
		}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #guo #First General Election: Commies wins (Commies support greater than KMT and CDL/CNSP, GAME OVER LOL)
	id = rcmchina_elections.4
	title = rcmchina_elections.4.t
	desc = rcmchina_elections.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_assembly_china
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rcmchina_elections.4.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		#country_event = rcmchina_elections_alt.4
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PRC_was_player_can_usurp_CHI
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = Root.core_states
					add_core_of = event_target:WTT_communist_china
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
					event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			
			root = {#guo
					every_character = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = former_communist_forces
					}
					set_nationality = event_target:WTT_communist_china
					}
					
					every_unit_leader = {
					limit = {
						has_unit_leader_flag = former_communist_forces
					}
					set_nationality = event_target:WTT_communist_china
					}
					
					every_army_leader = {
					limit = {
						has_unit_leader_flag = former_communist_forces
					}
					set_nationality = event_target:WTT_communist_china
					}
					
					event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
						create_country_leader = { #Safe because Sokolovsky doesn't exist ingame
							name="毛泽东"
							picture = "gfx/leaders/PRC/maozedong1949.jpg"
							ideology = maoism
							desc=prc_mao_zedong_desc
							traits = { cornered_fox tiancaidezhanluejia tiancaidesixiangjia youjizhandashi hero_of_the_peasantry_MAO red_sun_of_the_people }
						}
						promote_character = prc_mao_zedong
					}
			}
			
			event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
				change_tag_from = ROOT				
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = CONGRATS_YOU_SUBVERT_CHINA_WITHOUT_CIVIL_WAR
		}
		event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
			if = {#guo
			limit = { country_exists = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader }
			annex_country = {
				target = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader transfer_troops = yes
			}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = PRC_Establish_state_or_independent_government }
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = PRC_lianhezhengfu
			}
		}
		
		if = {#guo
		limit = { tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china has_global_flag = CPC_candidate_is_PRC_zhou_enlai }
			retire_country_leader = yes
			promote_character = PRC_zhou_enlai
			add_mao_advisor_trait = yes
		}
	}
}

#Commie coup when too popular
add_namespace = rcmchina_elections_coup
country_event = { #First General Election: Commies wins (Commies support greater than KMT and CDL/CNSP, GAME OVER LOL)
	id = rcmchina_elections_coup.4
	title = rcmchina_elections_coup.4.t
	desc = rcmchina_elections_coup.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_assembly_china
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
		has_idea = CHI_communist_in_government
		communism > 0.4
		neutrality < 0.25
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3	
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina_elections_coup.4.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			set_nationality = event_target:WTT_communist_china
		}
		#set_global_flag = PRC_was_player_can_usurp_CHI
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PRC_was_player_can_usurp_CHI
			}
			
			hidden_effect = {
				for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = Root.core_states
					add_core_of = event_target:WTT_communist_china
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
					event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
				change_tag_from = ROOT				
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = CONGRATS_YOU_SUBVERT_CHINA_WITHOUT_CIVIL_WAR
		}
		event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT transfer_troops = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = PRC_Establish_state_or_independent_government }
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = New_ROC
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = rcmchina_elections.8.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = democratic
			name = CHI_neutrality_party
			long_name = CHI_neutrality_party_long
		}
		#custom_effect_tooltip = KMT_become_ruling_party_politics_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CKS_leads_KMT
			}
			retire_ideology_leader = democratic
			CHI_chiang_kai_shek = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = sanmin_constitutional_government
						desc=POLITICS_CHIANG_KAISHEK_DESC #guo
						traits = {
							generallissimo
							
							junduiguanlian qinliqinwei kmt_zongcai #guo
						}
					} 
				}
				add_trait = {
					ideology = sanmin_constitutional_government
					trait = generallissimo
			    }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = HYQ_leads_KMT
			}
			CHI_he_yingqin = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = sanmin_constitutional_government
						traits = {
							army_chief_organizational_3 #guo
							generallissimo
							
							
						}
					} 
				}
				add_trait = {
					ideology = sanmin_constitutional_government
					trait = generallissimo
			    }
			}
		}
		clear_prvious_election_flags = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				months = 46 id = rcmchina_nomination_convention_future.1
			}
		}
	}
}

#NOMINATION, first general election
add_namespace = rcmchina_nomination_convention
country_event = { #[Original KMT leader] or Sun Fo?
	id = rcmchina_nomination_convention.1
	title = rcmchina_nomination_convention.1.t
	desc = rcmchina_nomination_convention.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_sun_fo
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rcmchina_nomination_convention.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		#custom_effect_tooltip = CKS_or_HYQ_becomes_candidate_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				or = { has_country_flag = CKS_leads_KMT CKS_in_charge = yes }#guo
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = CKS_becomes_candidate_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				or = { has_country_flag = CKS_leads_KMT and = { TAG = event_target:WTT_communist_china has_country_leader = { ruling_only = no character = CHI_he_yingqin } } }#guo
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = HYQ_becomes_candidate_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = cdl_founded
			}
			country_event = rcmchina_nomination_convention.3
			else = {
				country_event = rcmchina_nomination_convention.2
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina_nomination_convention.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = sun_fo_becomes_candidate_tt
		set_country_flag = KMT_candidate_is_sun_fo
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = cdl_founded
			}
			country_event = rcmchina_nomination_convention.3
			else = {
				country_event = rcmchina_nomination_convention.2
			}
		}
	}
}

#NOMINATION, future general election
add_namespace = rcmchina_nomination_convention_future
country_event = { #[Original KMT leader] or Sun Fo?
	id = rcmchina_nomination_convention_future.1
	title = rcmchina_nomination_convention_future.1.t
	desc = rcmchina_nomination_convention_future.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_sun_fo
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rcmchina_nomination_convention_future.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		#custom_effect_tooltip = CKS_or_HYQ_becomes_candidate_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				or = { has_country_flag = CKS_leads_KMT CKS_in_charge = yes }#guo
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = CKS_becomes_candidate_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				or = { has_country_flag = CKS_leads_KMT and = { TAG = event_target:WTT_communist_china has_country_leader = { ruling_only = no character = CHI_he_yingqin } } }#guo
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = HYQ_becomes_candidate_tt
		}
		#########################
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = cdl_founded
			}
			country_event = rcmchina_nomination_convention_future.3
			else = {
				country_event = rcmchina_nomination_convention_future.2
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina_nomination_convention_future.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = sun_fo_becomes_candidate_tt
		set_country_flag = KMT_candidate_is_sun_fo
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = cdl_founded
			}
			country_event = rcmchina_nomination_convention_future.3
			else = {
				country_event = rcmchina_nomination_convention_future.2
			}
		}
	}
}

#DEMAND OVERLORDSHIP
add_namespace = rcmchina_overlordship
country_event = {
	id = rcmchina_overlordship.1
	title = rcmchina_overlordship.1.t
	desc = rcmchina_overlordship.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_public_hearing_2

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmchina_overlordship.1"}

	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rcmchina_overlordship.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		CHI = {
			country_event = rcmchina_overlordship.2
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = JAP
				NOT = {
					tag = MAN
				}
				OR = {
					tag = HPC
					tag = EHB
					tag = ECA
					tag = NSG
					tag = SCG
					is_literally_china = yes
				}
			}
			get_current_government_type = yes
			end_puppet = PREV
			CHI = {
				puppet = PREV
			}
			restore_previous_government_type = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmchina_overlordship.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		CHI = {
			country_event = rcmchina_overlordship.3
		}
	}
}
