#Q constitutionalization arose again
country_event = {
	id = rcmchina.368
	title = rcmchina.368.t
	desc = rcmchina.368.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_political_hearing

	#immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rcmchina.368"}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		NOT = {
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = no_longer_affected_by_pressure_flag
					has_completed_focus = CHI_suppress_constitutionalist_pressure
					has_completed_focus = CHI_constitution_focus
					has_war_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china
					has_active_mission = CHI_tension_with_communists
					has_active_mission = RCM_constitutionalization_pressure
					has_defensive_war_with = JAP				
					has_completed_focus = CHI_declare_martial_law_focus
					has_completed_focus = CHI_cult_of_chiang_kai_shek
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							has_completed_focus = CHI_support_kmt_opposition_focus
						}
						any_enemy_country = {
							OR = {
								is_neighbor_of = ROOT
								any_allied_country = {
									is_subject_of = PREV
									is_neighbor_of = ROOT
								}
							}
							OR = {
								is_major = yes
								tag = JAP
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rcmchina.368.a
		activate_mission = RCM_constitutionalization_pressure		
	}
}

	id = rcmchina.369
	title = rcmchina.369.t
	desc = rcmchina.369.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_battle_of_wuhan_3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		trigger = {
			tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
		}
		name = rcmchina.369.a
		set_capital = { state = 1034 }	
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					owns_state = 605
				}
				any_other_country = {
					original_tag = SIC
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					owns_state = 605
					controls_state = 605
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 605
		}	
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			original_tag = SIC
		}
		name = rcmchina.369.b
		effect_tooltip = {
            event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
				set_capital = { state = 1034 }	
				transfer_state = 605
			}
		}	
	}
}

	desc = rcmchina.372.d

	}

		name = rcmchina.372.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = CHI_chiang_kai_shek
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			kill_country_leader = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = wang_ruling_idea
		hidden_effect = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = chiang
	}
}

#Yellow river is flooded, people not happy
# Event complaining about unneeded flooding
add_namespace = rcmchina_flood_yellow_river
country_event = {
	id = rcmchina_flood_yellow_river.1
	title = rcmchina_flood_yellow_river.1.t
	desc = rcmchina_flood_yellow_river.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_polderen
	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = CHI_YEL_inundation_lines_flooded
		OR = {
			607 = {
				controller = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 607
					OR = {
						tag = ROOT
						#is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			1043 = {
				controller = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 1043
					OR = {
						tag = ROOT
						#is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			606 = {
				controller = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 606
					OR = {
						tag = ROOT
						#is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			598 = {
				controller = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 598
					OR = {
						tag = ROOT
						#is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = CHI_YEL_inundation_lines_flooded_relief_or_propa_timer }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = CHI_YEL_draining_in_progress }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 60
	}

	immediate = {
	}
	
	# Use as propaganda
	option = {

		trigger = {
			has_war = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 
				is_literally_china = yes #the chinese saves their own
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_full_control_of_state = 606
			}
			add_political_power = 5
			add_war_support = 0.005

				}
				damage_building = {
					type = arms_factory
					damage = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_full_control_of_state = 598
			}
			add_political_power = 5
			add_war_support = 0.005
			598 = {
				damage_building = {
					type = infrastructure
					damage = 3
				}

					type = industrial_complex
					damage = 1.5
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = arms_factory
					damage = 1.5
				}
			}		
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_full_control_of_state = 1043
			}
			add_political_power = 5
			add_war_support = 0.005
			1043 = {
				damage_building = {
					type = infrastructure
					damage = 1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_full_control_of_state = 607
			}
			add_political_power = 5
			add_war_support = 0.005
			607 = {
				damage_building = {
					type = infrastructure
					damage = 2
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = industrial_complex
					damage = 0.5
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = arms_factory
					damage = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Focus on relief 
	option = {
		name = rcmchina_flood_yellow_river.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10 #the chinese saves their own
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 
				NOT = {
					is_literally_china = yes
				}
			}
		}

			limit = {
				has_full_control_of_state = 606
			}
			add_political_power = -5
			add_war_support = 0.003
			add_stability = 0.005
			custom_effect_tooltip = gain_base_supp_cond_n1dot5_tt
			add_to_variable = {
				Root.supply_condition_base = -1.5
			}
			606 = {
				damage_building = {
					type = infrastructure
					damage = 0.5
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = industrial_complex
					damage = 0.15
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = arms_factory
					damage = 0.15
				}
			}
		}

			}
			add_political_power = -5
			add_war_support = 0.003
			add_stability = 0.005
			custom_effect_tooltip = gain_base_supp_cond_n1dot5_tt

			}
			598 = {
				damage_building = {

					damage = 1
				}

				}
				damage_building = {
					type = arms_factory
					damage = 0.3
				}
			}		
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_full_control_of_state = 1043
			}

	desc = nw_barracks_of_high_command.2.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_mong_army_01

	immediate = {
	}

	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = nw_barracks_of_high_command.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = {
						tag = NEA
					}
					num_of_controlled_states > 1
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 756
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = {
						tag = NEA
					}
				}
				country_exists = XSM
			}
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						tag = GSM
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = XSM
						}
					}
					XSM_ma_buqing = {
						set_nationality = XSM
					}
					XSM_ma_chengxiang = {
						set_nationality = XSM
					}
				}
				else = {
					every_unit_leader = {
						set_nationality = XSM
					}
				}
			    transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = XSM         # the recipient
					size = 0.5          # [0,1] Default value for the ratio below if they are not specified
					army_ratio = 1       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for army
					#stockpile_ratio = 0.3  # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for the stockpiled equipment and fuel
					#navy_ratio = 0.2       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for navy
					#air_ratio = 0.4        # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for air
					keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { # Trigger for unit leaders to remain with the original country
						always = yes
					}
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = FROM transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			FROM = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = ROOT
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = FROM transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# Form Indian Liberation Army
country_event = {
	id = RCM_old_china.1022
	title = RCM_old_china.1022.t
	desc = RCM_old_china.1022.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_bose
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = RCM_old_china.1022.a
		RAJ = {
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = fascism
				size = 0.2
				capital = 430
				states = { 288 640 430 434 432 1056 1057 }
			}
			add_stability = -0.2
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = RAJ
					not = { tag = RAJ }
				}
				load_focus_tree = warlord_generic_communist
				save_global_event_target_as = RAJ_CHI_puppet
				event_target:RAJ_CHI_puppet = {
					PREV = {
						add_to_war = {
							targeted_alliance = CHI
							enemy = PREV
						}
					}
				}					
				JAP = {
					add_to_faction = PREV
				}
				for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = RAJ.core_states
					THIS = {
						add_core_of = event_target:RAJ_CHI_puppet
					}
				}
				get_current_government_type = yes
				CHI = {

				}

					name = azad_hind_party
					long_name = azad_hind_party_long
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = azad_hind

				create_corps_commander = {

					traits = {}

					defense_skill = 2

				}
				create_corps_commander = {

					portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/RAJ/GFX_portrait_Shah_Nawaz_Khan.dds"
					traits = {}
					skill = 2

				}

				create_corps_commander = {

				}

				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit =  {
				CHI = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality

			}
		}
